"Gimbap and norimaki now refer to distinct dishes in Japan and Korea: the former called kimupapu (キムパプ) in Japanese and the latter called gimchobap (ㄱㅣㅁㅊㅗㅂㅏㅂ; ""gim sushi"") or norimaki (ㄴㅗㄹㅣㅁㅏㅋㅣ) in Korean. Gimbap usually contains more ingredients and is seasoned with sesame oil, while norimaki is rolled with fewer ingredients and is seasoned with rice vinegar."
